# Longus Cattus' Notes:
# Most dates from before the Asuka Period are traditional and shouldn't be taken literally.
# If you notice any errors, please feel free to let me know on the AEP Discord: https://discord.gg/avM245rrXa.
# 飛鳥時代以前の日付は多くが伝統的なものであり、厳密に受け取る必要はありません。
# もし誤りを見つけた場合は、お気軽にAEP Discord（https://discord.gg/avM245rrXa）までお知らせください。

############################
### Imperial Family 皇室 ###
############################

	name = Kamuyamatoiwarebikonomikoto # 神日本磐余彦天皇

	religion = shinto
	culture = yamato
	diplomacy = 5
	martial = 10
	stewardship = 7
	intrigue = 4

	prowess = 13

	trait = brave
	trait = zealous
	trait = diligent
	trait = holy_warrior

		birth = yes

			add_character_flag = has_scripted_appearance
		}	
	}

	}
}

kawachiminamoto_yoshiie = {
	name = Yoshiie # 義家
	dynasty_house = house_kawachigenji
	religion = shinto
	culture = yamato 
	
	diplomacy = 5
	martial = 10
	stewardship = 6
	intrigue = 4
	learning = 7
	prowess = 13
	trait = education_martial_4
	trait = brave
	trait = ambitious
	trait = diligent
	trait = holy_warrior
	trait = gallant
	trait = strong
	disallow_random_traits = yes
	
	father = kawachiminamoto_yoriyoshi
	mother = taira_naokata_musume
	1039.1.1 = {
		birth = yes
		effect = {
			add_character_flag = has_scripted_appearance
		}	
	}
	1063.1.1 = {
		give_nickname = nick_hachimantaro # 八幡太郎
	}
	1066.9.15 = {
		set_relation_rival = { target = character:yamatominamoto_yoritoshi reason = rival_historical }
		effect = {
			#Yoshiie and his cousin Yoritoshi had competing ambitions to subdue the Emishi to their north, later realized during the Enkyu Ezo War.
			add_pressed_claim = title:c_nukanobu
			add_pressed_claim = title:c_tsugaru
			add_pressed_claim = title:c_hinai
		}
	}
	1106.8.4 = {
		death = yes
	}
	dna = kawachiminamoto_yoshiie_dna_entry
}

	name = Benkei # 弁慶

	culture = yamato

	diplomacy=2
	martial=11
	stewardship=2
	intrigue=4
	learning=6
	prowess=12

	trait = brave

	trait = humble
	trait = gallant
	trait = strong
	trait = intellect_good_1
	trait = education_martial_prowess_3
	trait = unyielding_defender
	disallow_random_traits = yes

		birth = yes
	}
	1165.1.1 = {
		trait = devoted
	}

			death_reason = death_battle
